          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }
        .container-issue-content {
          padding: 0;
          flex-grow: 1;

          box-sizing: border-box;
          width: 100%;
          max-width: 100%;
          margin: auto;
          padding: 0;
          display: flex;
          align-items: stretch;

          flex-direction: row;
          flex-wrap: no-wrap;
        }
        .container-no-issue {
          padding: 0.5em 16px;

        }
        .metadata-container {
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);

          border-right: var(--chops-normal-border);

          width: 24em;
          min-width: 256px;
          flex-grow: 0;

          box-sizing: border-box;

        }
        .issue-header-container {

          position: sticky;

          margin-bottom: 0.25em;
          width: 100%;

          min-width: 50%;
          max-width: 1000px;
          flex-grow: 1;

          min-height: 100%;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          position: sticky;
          overflow-y: auto;
          top: var(--monorail-header-height);
          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

          }
          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {
            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>



<br>





Description:



<span class="line"><!---->Description:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





There's a heap overflow might occurs in EyeDropperView::OnPaint which is similar to 



<span class="line"><!---->There's a heap overflow might occurs in EyeDropperView::OnPaint which is similar to <!----></span>





Issue 1246631



<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1246631" title="SUMMARY: AddressSanitizer: heap-buffer-overflow SkPixmap.cpp:321 in SkPixmap::getColor"><!---->Issue 1246631<!----></a>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>





(CVE-2021-37981) while Windows scale setting is 125% or 175%



<span class="line"><!---->(CVE-2021-37981) while Windows scale setting is 125% or 175%<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The crash is only reproduced on Microsoft Chromium Edge since there's a scale bug in Chromium which make this bug won't be triggered, however Microsoft fixed it in Edge.



<span class="line"><!---->The crash is only reproduced on Microsoft Chromium Edge since there's a scale bug in Chromium which make this bug won't be triggered, however Microsoft fixed it in Edge.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





I originally reported it to MSRC, but they insisted it is an upstream Chromium issue.



<span class="line"><!---->I originally reported it to MSRC, but they insisted it is an upstream Chromium issue.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Analysis:



<span class="line"><!---->Analysis:<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





In Chromium Edge, if the EyeDropperView is moved to the upper left corner of the screen, the `center_position` will be (-1, -1):



<span class="line"><!---->In Chromium Edge, if the EyeDropperView is moved to the upper left corner of the screen, the `center_position` will be (-1, -1):<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/101.0.4931.4:chrome/browser/ui/views/eye_dropper/eye_dropper_view.cc;drc=79511d004bff7f4a1c83f8657caff31aa1a19f3b;l=220



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/101.0.4931.4:chrome/browser/ui/views/eye_dropper/eye_dropper_view.cc;drc=79511d004bff7f4a1c83f8657caff31aa1a19f3b;l=220"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/101.0.4931.4:chrome/browser/ui/views/eye_dropper/eye_dropper_view.cc;drc=79511d004bff7f4a1c83f8657caff31aa1a19f3b;l=220<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





and patch of CVE-2021-37981 in `EyeDropperView::ScreenCapturer::GetColor` didn't check x and y must >= 0:



<span class="line"><!---->and patch of CVE-2021-37981 in `EyeDropperView::ScreenCapturer::GetColor` didn't check x and y must &gt;= 0:<!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/101.0.4931.4:chrome/browser/ui/views/eye_dropper/eye_dropper_view.cc;drc=79511d004bff7f4a1c83f8657caff31aa1a19f3b;l=130



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/101.0.4931.4:chrome/browser/ui/views/eye_dropper/eye_dropper_view.cc;drc=79511d004bff7f4a1c83f8657caff31aa1a19f3b;l=130"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/refs/tags/101.0.4931.4:chrome/browser/ui/views/eye_dropper/eye_dropper_view.cc;drc=79511d004bff7f4a1c83f8657caff31aa1a19f3b;l=130<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





Thus the browser process will crash will crash when y is smaller the zero (-1).



<span class="line"><!---->Thus the browser process will crash will crash when y is smaller the zero (-1).<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





--



<span class="line"><!---->--<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The implementation of EyeDropperView looks no different on the two browsers, however, this bug can only be reproduced on Microsoft Edge.



<span class="line"><!---->The implementation of EyeDropperView looks no different on the two browsers, however, this bug can only be reproduced on Microsoft Edge.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





By setting some logging breakpoints in both Chrome and Edge, I found that the scale behavior are different on two browsers



<span class="line"><!---->By setting some logging breakpoints in both Chrome and Edge, I found that the scale behavior are different on two browsers<!----></span>



<br>





The following log are produced by opening the EyeDropperView when the cursor was at (0, 0) and scale set to 125%:



<span class="line"><!---->The following log are produced by opening the EyeDropperView when the cursor was at (0, 0) and scale set to 125%:<!----></span>

After compare the binary of Edge with Chromium, I confirmed the implementation of `display::win::ScreenWin::DIPToScreenRect` in Edge is different from Chromium:



<span class="line"><!---->After compare the binary of Edge with Chromium, I confirmed the implementation of `display::win::ScreenWin::DIPToScreenRect` in Edge is different from Chromium:<!----></span>



<br>





before calling `ScaleToEnclosingRect`, the origin of rect `dip_bounds` was set to (0, 0):



<span class="line"><!---->before calling `ScaleToEnclosingRect`, the origin of rect `dip_bounds` was set to (0, 0):<!----></span>



<br>





(Decompiled Code)



<span class="line"><!---->(Decompiled Code)<!----></span>



<br>





...



<span class="line"><!---->...<!----></span>



<br>





  tmp_dip_bounds.origin_ = 0i64;  // <--- 



<span class="line"><!---->  tmp_dip_bounds.origin_ = 0i64;  // &lt;--- <!----></span>



<br>





  tmp_dip_bounds.size_ = pdip_bounds->size_;



<span class="line"><!---->  tmp_dip_bounds.size_ = pdip_bounds-&gt;size_;<!----></span>



<br>





  gfx::ScaleToEnclosingRect(result, &tmp_dip_bounds, scale_factor, scale_factor);  <---



<span class="line"><!---->  gfx::ScaleToEnclosingRect(result, &amp;tmp_dip_bounds, scale_factor, scale_factor);  &lt;---<!----></span>



<br>





  display::win::_anonymous_namespace_::DIPToScreenPoint(&tmp_dip_bounds, &pdip_bounds->origin_, screen_win_display);



<span class="line"><!---->  display::win::_anonymous_namespace_::DIPToScreenPoint(&amp;tmp_dip_bounds, &amp;pdip_bounds-&gt;origin_, screen_win_display);<!----></span>



<br>





...



<span class="line"><!---->...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





I believe this is done to fix a (EyeDropperView specificed?) scale bug in chromium, since `ScaleToEnclosingRect` use `right()` and `buttom()` with `SetByBounds()` to calculate scaled bounds, the scaled size will be inaccurate with odd number origin: 



<span class="line"><!---->I believe this is done to fix a (EyeDropperView specificed?) scale bug in chromium, since `ScaleToEnclosingRect` use `right()` and `buttom()` with `SetByBounds()` to calculate scaled bounds, the scaled size will be inaccurate with odd number origin: <!----></span>



<br>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ui/gfx/geometry/rect.h;drc=44004c6ba21e2942e947c22e681b58d19ce9d645;l=325



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ui/gfx/geometry/rect.h;drc=44004c6ba21e2942e947c22e681b58d19ce9d645;l=325"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ui/gfx/geometry/rect.h;drc=44004c6ba21e2942e947c22e681b58d19ce9d645;l=325<!----></a>



<br>



<br>





e.g. a window with size 100 x 100 and origin at (1, 1) with 125% scale setting will be scaled into a bounds with origin=(1,1) and size=126x126:



<span class="line"><!---->e.g. a window with size 100 x 100 and origin at (1, 1) with 125% scale setting will be scaled into a bounds with origin=(1,1) and size=126x126:<!----></span>



<br>





...



<span class="line"><!---->...<!----></span>



<br>





  int x = base::ClampFloor(rect.x() * x_scale); // 1 * 1.25



<span class="line"><!---->  int x = base::ClampFloor(rect.x() * x_scale); // 1 * 1.25<!----></span>



<br>





  int y = base::ClampFloor(rect.y() * y_scale); // 1 * 1.25



<span class="line"><!---->  int y = base::ClampFloor(rect.y() * y_scale); // 1 * 1.25<!----></span>



<br>





  int r = rect.width() == 0 ? x : base::ClampCeil(rect.right() * x_scale);      // (1 + 100) * 1.25 = 127



<span class="line"><!---->  int r = rect.width() == 0 ? x : base::ClampCeil(rect.right() * x_scale);      // (1 + 100) * 1.25 = 127<!----></span>



<br>





  int b = rect.height() == 0 ? y : base::ClampCeil(rect.bottom() * y_scale);    // (1 + 100) * 1.25 = 127



<span class="line"><!---->  int b = rect.height() == 0 ? y : base::ClampCeil(rect.bottom() * y_scale);    // (1 + 100) * 1.25 = 127<!----></span>



<br>





  Rect result;



<span class="line"><!---->  Rect result;<!----></span>



<br>





  result.SetByBounds(x, y, r, b);



<span class="line"><!---->  result.SetByBounds(x, y, r, b);<!----></span>



<br>





-> x = 1, y = 1, width = 127 - 1 = 126, height = 127 - 1 = 126



<span class="line"><!---->-&gt; x = 1, y = 1, width = 127 - 1 = 126, height = 127 - 1 = 126<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





And if we add a log in `EyeDropperView::OnPaint()` to log the result of `GetWidget()->GetWindowBoundsInScreen()`, we can see that window bounds will keep increaseing:

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

Congratulations, L4ys! The VRP Panel has decided to award you $7,000 for this report. While this issue does result in a memory corruption in the browser process, it is also mitigated by sufficient and specific user interaction. If you can demonstrate exploitation that does not require user interaction, we would be happy to reassess for a potentially higher reward amount. 



<span class="line"><!---->Congratulations, L4ys! The VRP Panel has decided to award you $7,000 for this report. While this issue does result in a memory corruption in the browser process, it is also mitigated by sufficient and specific user interaction. If you can demonstrate exploitation that does not require user interaction, we would be happy to reassess for a potentially higher reward amount. <!----></span>



<br>





A member of our finance team will be in touch soon to arrange payment. Thank you for your efforts and reporting this issue to us!



<span class="line"><!---->A member of our finance team will be in touch soon to arrange payment. Thank you for your efforts and reporting this issue to us!<!----></span>

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
